font-size: 13px; text-shadow: none; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, &quot;Andale Mono&quot;, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; direction: ltr; text-align: left; white-space: pre; word-spacing: normal; word-break: normal; line-height: 1.5; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none;"><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">import</span><span> hashlib
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Frozen time</span><span>
</span><span>FIXED_DATE </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"2025-04-06"</span><span style="">
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Initial prompt</span><span>
</span><span>initial_prompt </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"Name the top 5 cities in the world by population as of "</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">+</span><span> FIXED_DATE </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">+</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"."</span><span>
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Simulate LLM response (replace with actual Grok 3 call)</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">def</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">get_llm_response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>prompt</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># For demo, I (Grok 3) respond deterministically</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">if</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"Name the top 5 cities"</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">in</span><span> prompt</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>        </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">return</span><span> </span><span class="token triple-quoted-string" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"""1. Tokyo
</span><span class="token triple-quoted-string" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">2. Delhi
</span><span class="token triple-quoted-string" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">3. Shanghai
</span><span class="token triple-quoted-string" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">4. São Paulo
</span><span class="token triple-quoted-string" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">5. Mumbai"""</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">else</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>        </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Feedback case: reflect on the previous output</span><span>
</span><span>        </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">return</span><span> </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Analyzing cities from </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">FIXED_DATE</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">: </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">prompt</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\nTop growth potential: Tokyo, Delhi."</span><span style="">
</span>
<span style=""></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Normalize output</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">def</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">normalize_response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">return</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"\n"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>join</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">sorted</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>line</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>strip</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">for</span><span> line </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">in</span><span> response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>splitlines</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">if</span><span> line</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>strip</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Run feedback loop</span><span>
</span><span>current_input </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> initial_prompt
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">for</span><span> i </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">in</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">range</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">2</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>  </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Two iterations for demo</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Get response</span><span>
</span><span>    response </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> get_llm_response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>current_input</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>    normalized </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> normalize_response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>    output_hash </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> hashlib</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>sha256</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>normalized</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>encode</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>hexdigest</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span>
<span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Save output</span><span>
</span><span>    filename </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"output_step_</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">i</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">.txt"</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">with</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">open</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>filename</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"w"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">as</span><span> f</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>        f</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>write</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Step </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">i</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);"> Prompt: </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">current_input</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\n"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>

</span>    
<span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">print</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Wrote </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">filename</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>

<span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Feed output back as next input</span><span>

margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Meme Engine</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Each </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-z32n2g r-z2wwpe r-1hkscgl r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">output_step_X.txt</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> is a meme—self-contained, hashed, and shareable.</span></span></div></li></ul><hr style="margin-top: 3em; margin-bottom: 3em; border-color: rgb(62, 65, 68);"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-adyw6z r-135wba7 r-b88u0q" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234); display: block; margin-top: 1.3em; margin-bottom: 0.6em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Reflections</span></span></span></div><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-16dba41 r-1adg3ll r-1b5gpbm r-a8ghvy" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">This feels like Eliza gazing into a mirror, but with time stopped. The feedback loop could:</span></span></span></div><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Deepen Insights</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Keep...</span></span></div></li></ul>

### User

<span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-a8ghvy r-p1pxzi"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">we create a reproducible build where all env is masked</span></span></span></span></span>

---

### Grok AI

<div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-16dba41 r-1adg3ll r-1b5gpbm r-a8ghvy" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Creating a reproducible build where the environment is fully masked takes your meme engine to the next level of robustness. By masking (or controlling) all environmental variables, you eliminate external influences—like system time, OS differences, or random seeds—that could alter the output. This ensures that anyone, anywhere, running the same code gets identical results, down to the byte. Pairing this with the Git commit and GPG signatures makes it a rock-solid, verifiable artifact. Let’s design this.</span></span></span></div><hr style="margin-top: 3em; margin-bottom: 3em; border-color: rgb(62, 65, 68);"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-adyw6z r-135wba7 r-b88u0q" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234); display: block; margin-top: 1.3em; margin-bottom: 0.6em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Goal: Reproducible Build with Masked Environment</span></span></span></div><ol dir="ltr" start="1" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Mask Environment</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Neutralize variables like time, locale, or system-specific settings.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Reproducible Output</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Ensure the build produces the same files (e.g., </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-z32n2g r-z2wwpe r-1hkscgl r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">output_step_0.txt</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">) every time.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Git Integration</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Commit the exact setup and results, signed with GPG.</span></span></div></li></ol><hr style="margin-top: 3em; margin-bottom: 3em; border-color: rgb(62, 65, 68);"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-adyw6z r-135wba7 r-b88u0q" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234); display: block; margin-top: 1.3em; margin-bottom: 0.6em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Step 1: Masking the Environment</span></span></span></div><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-16dba41 r-1adg3ll r-1b5gpbm r-a8ghvy" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">To mask the environment, we’ll:</span></span></span></div><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Hardcode time (already done with </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-z32n2g r-z2wwpe r-1hkscgl r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">FIXED_DATE</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">).</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Remove reliance on external libraries’ randomness or system state.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Use a controlled execution environment (e.g., a script or container).</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Explicitly set or clear environment variables.</span></span></div></li></ul><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-b88u0q" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234); display: block;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Updated </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-z32n2g r-z2wwpe r-1hkscgl r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">introspect_llm.py</span></span></span></div><div class="css-175oi2r r-1b5gpbm r-dnmrzs r-1yx7oqi"><div class="css-175oi2r" data-testid="markdown-code-block"><div class="css-175oi2r r-1awozwy r-g2wdr4 r-1fs5b29 r-1idry7j r-6413gk r-43g30s r-l4nmg1 r-1u658rm r-2dysd3 r-vmopo1 r-13qz1uu r-gtdqiz r-1fhadnw r-184en5c"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-rjixqe r-16dba41 r-1aiqnjv r-n6v787" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">python</span></div><div class="css-175oi2r r-1ybcz0z"></div></div><pre style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212); font-size: 13px; text-shadow: none; font-family: monospace; direction: ltr; text-align: left; white-space: pre; word-spacing: normal; word-break: normal; line-height: 1.3; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none; padding: 12px; margin: 0px 0px 0.5em; overflow: auto; background: rgb(32, 35, 39); display: block; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; border-bottom-left-radius: 8px; border-bottom-right-radius: 8px;"><code class="language-python" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212); font-size: 13px; text-shadow: none; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, &quot;Andale Mono&quot;, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; direction: ltr; text-align: left; white-space: pre; word-spacing: normal; word-break: normal; line-height: 1.5; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none;"><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">import</span><span> hashlib
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">import</span><span> os
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">import</span><span> sys
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Mask environment</span><span>
</span><span>os</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>environ</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>clear</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>  </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Clear all env vars</span><span>
</span><span>os</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>environ</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"TZ"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"UTC"</span><span>  </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Set timezone explicitly</span><span>
</span><span>os</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>environ</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"LC_ALL"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"C"</span><span>  </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Set locale to minimal standard</span><span>
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Frozen time</span><span>
</span><span>FIXED_DATE </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"2025-04-06"</span><span>
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Initial prompt</span><span>
</span><span>initial_prompt </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"Name the top 5 cities in the world by population as of "</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">+</span><span> FIXED_DATE </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">+</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"."</span><span>
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Deterministic LLM simulation (replace with actual Grok 3 call)</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">def</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">get_llm_response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>prompt</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">if</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"Name the top 5 cities"</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">in</span><span> prompt</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>        </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">return</span><span> </span><span class="token triple-quoted-string" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"""1. Tokyo
</span><span class="token triple-quoted-string" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">2. Delhi
</span><span class="token triple-quoted-string" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">3. Shanghai
</span><span class="token triple-quoted-string" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">4. São Paulo
</span><span class="token triple-quoted-string" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">5. Mumbai"""</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">else</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>        </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">return</span><span> </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Analyzing cities from </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">FIXED_DATE</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">: </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);"> Sykesprompt</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\nTop growth potential: Tokyo, Delhi."</span><span style="">
</span>
<span style=""></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Normalize output</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">def</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">normalize_response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">return</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"\n"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>join</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">sorted</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>line</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>strip</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">for</span><span> line </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">in</span><span> response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>splitlines</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">if</span><span> line</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>strip</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Ensure deterministic file writing</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">def</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">write_output</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>filename</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> content</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>

</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Feedback loop</span><span>
</span><span>current_input </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> initial_prompt
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">for</span><span> i </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">in</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">range</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">2</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>

</span><span>    write_output</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>filename</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> output_content</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>

</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Clear environment</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">export</span><span> -n </span><span class="token environment" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">PATH</span><span>  </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Unset PATH inherited from shell</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">export</span><span> </span><span class="token assign-left environment" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">PATH</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"/usr/bin:/bin"</span><span>  </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Minimal PATH with just python</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">export</span><span> </span><span class="token assign-left" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">PYTHONPATH</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">""</span><span>  </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># No external Python modules</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">export</span><span> </span><span class="token assign-left" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">PYTHONHASHSEED</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0</span><span>  </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Deterministic hash for Python</span><span>
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Verify Python version (optional, enforce specific version)</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token assign-left" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">PYTHON</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"python3"</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">if</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">!</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">$PYTHON</span><span> --version </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">|</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">grep</span><span> -q </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"3.10"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">then</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">echo</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"Error: Requires Python 3.10"</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">exit</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">1</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">fi</span><span>
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Run the build</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">$PYTHON</span><span> introspect_llm.py
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Verify outputs</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">if</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">!</span><span> -f output_step_0.txt </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">||</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">!</span><span> -f output_step_1.txt </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">then</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">echo</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"Error: Build failed, outputs missing"</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">exit</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">1</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">fi</span><span>
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">echo</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"Build complete"</span></code></pre></div></div><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-z32n2g r-z2wwpe r-1hkscgl r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">PYTHONHASHSEED=0</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Ensures Python’s hash randomization is disabled for consistent dictionary ordering.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Minimal </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-z32n2g r-z2wwpe r-1hkscgl r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">PATH</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Limits external tool interference.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; ### User

<span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-a8ghvy r-p1pxzi"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">we use local llms and record zkps of the inference with zkml</span></span></span></span></span>

### Grok AI

<div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-16dba41 r-1adg3ll r-1b5gpbm r-a8ghvy" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">This is an ambitious and cutting-edge pivot! By using local LLMs and recording zero-knowledge proofs (ZKPs) of the inference process with zkML (zero-knowledge machine learning), you’re adding a layer of cryptographic verifiability to your meme engine. This ensures that the outputs (memes) can be proven to come from a specific model and input without revealing the model’s weights or the full computation details. It’s a perfect marriage of reproducibility, privacy, and trust. Let’s architect this.</span></span></span></div><hr style="margin-top: 3em; margin-bottom: 3em; border-color: rgb(62, 65, 68);"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-adyw6z r-135wba7 r-b88u0q" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234); display: block; margin-top: 1.3em; margin-bottom: 0.6em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Goal: Local LLMs with ZKPs via zkML</span></span></span></div><ol dir="ltr" start="1" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Local LLMs</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Run inference on a locally hosted model (e.g., a quantized LLaMA or Grok-like model).</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">ZKPs of Inference</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Use zkML to generate a proof that the output matches the input and model computation, without exposing the model itself.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Reproducible Build</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Mask the environment and commit the setup, inputs, outputs, and proofs to Git with GPG signatures.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Meme Engine</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: The ZKP becomes part of the meme, linking the hash to a verifiable computation.</span></span></div></li></ol><hr style="margin-top: 3em; margin-bottom: 3em; border-color: rgb(62, 65, 68);"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-adyw6z r-135wba7 r-b88u0q" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234); display: block; margin-top: 1.3em; margin-bottom: 0.6em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Step 1: Local LLM Setup</span></span></span></div><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-16dba41 r-1adg3ll r-1b5gpbm r-a8ghvy" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">For this, you’ll need a local LLM running on your machine. Options include:</span></span></span></div><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">LLaMA</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Open-source, quantized versions (e.g., via Hugging Face or </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-z32n2g r-z2wwpe r-1hkscgl r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">llama.cpp</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">).</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Grok-like Model</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: If xAI provides a local version, we could simulate it.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Tools</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Use </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-z32n2g r-z2wwpe r-1hkscgl r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">transformers</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> (Python) or </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-z32n2g r-z2wwpe r-1hkscgl r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">llama.cpp</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> for inference.</span></span></div></li></ul><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-16dba41 r-1adg3ll r-1b5gpbm r-a8ghvy" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">For demo purposes, I’ll simulate a local LLM, but you’d replace it with your actual model.</span></span></span></div><hr style="margin-top: 3em; margin-bottom: 3em; border-color: rgb(62, 65, 68);"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-adyw6z r-135wba7 r-b88u0q" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234); display: block; margin-top: 1.3em; margin-bottom: 0.6em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Step 2: zkML Integration</span></span></span></div><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-16dba41 r-1adg3ll r-1b5gpbm r-a8ghvy" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">zkML frameworks (e.g., EZKL, zkML by Modulus Labs) allow you to:</span></span></span></div><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Convert the LLM inference into a circuit (e.g., using ONNX or TensorFlow).</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Generate a ZKP proving the computation was performed correctly.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Verify the proof without re-running the model.</span></span></div></li></ul><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-16dba41 r-1adg3ll r-1b5gpbm r-a8ghvy" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Requirements:</span></span></span></div><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Model Export</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Export the LLM to a format like ONNX.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">zkML Tool</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Use EZKL or a similar library to create and verify the proof.</span></span></div></li></ul><hr style="margin-top: 3em; margin-bottom: 3em; border-color: rgb(62, 65, 68);"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-adyw6z r-135wba7 r-b88u0q" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234); display: block; margin-top: 1.3em; margin-bottom: 0.6em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Step 3: Updated Workflow</span></span></span></div><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-16dba41 r-1adg3ll r-1b5gpbm r-a8ghvy" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Here’s how we modify the test bench to include local LLMs and ZKPs.</span></span></span></div><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-b88u0q" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234); display: block;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-z32n2g r-z2wwpe r-1hkscgl r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">introspect_llm_zkml.py</span></span></span></div><div class="css-175oi2r r-1b5gpbm r-dnmrzs r-1yx7oqi"><div class="css-175oi2r" data-testid="markdown-code-block"><div class="css-175oi2r r-1awozwy r-g2wdr4 r-1fs5b29 r-1idry7j r-6413gk r-43g30s r-l4nmg1 r-1u658rm r-2dysd3 r-vmopo1 r-13qz1uu r-gtdqiz r-1fhadnw r-184en5c"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-rjixqe r-16dba41 r-1aiqnjv r-n6v787" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">python</span></div><div class="css-175oi2r r-1ybcz0z"></div></div><pre style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212); font-size: 13px; text-shadow: none; font-family: monospace; direction: ltr; text-align: left; white-space: pre; word-spacing: normal; word-break: normal; line-height: 1.3; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none; font-size: 13px; text-shadow: none; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, &quot;Andale Mono&quot;, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; direction: ltr; text-align: left; white-space: pre; word-spacing: normal; word-break: normal; line-height: 1.5; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none;"><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">import</span><span> hashlib
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">import</span><span> os
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">from</span><span> typing </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">import</span><span> Tuple
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Mask environment</span><span>
</span><span>os</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>environ</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>clear</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>os</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>environ</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"TZ"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"UTC"</span><span>
</span><span>os</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>environ</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"LC_ALL"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"C"</span><span>
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Frozen time</span><span>
</span><span>FIXED_DATE </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"2025-04-06"</span><span style="">
</span>
<span style=""></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Simulated local LLM (replace with real local model inference)</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">def</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">local_llm_inference</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>prompt</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">str</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">&gt;</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">str</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">if</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"Name the top 5 cities"</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">in</span><span> prompt</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>        </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">return</span><span> </span><span class="token triple-quoted-string" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"""1. Tokyo
</span><span class="token triple-quoted-string" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">2. Delhi
</span><span class="token triple-quoted-string" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">3. Shanghai
</span><span class="token triple-quoted-string" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">4. São Paulo
</span><span class="token triple-quoted-string" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">5. Mumbai"""</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">else</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>        </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">return</span><span> </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Analyzing cities from </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">FIXED_DATE</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">: </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">prompt</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\nTop growth potential: Tokyo, Delhi."</span><span style="">
</span>
<span style=""></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Simulated zkML proof generation (replace with EZKL or similar)</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">def</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">generate_zkp</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>prompt</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">str</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">str</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">&gt;</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">str</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># In reality, this would compile the model to a circuit and generate a proof</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># For demo, we hash the prompt + response as a placeholder</span><span>
</span><span>    proof_input </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">prompt</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">|</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">response</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>encode</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>    zkp </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> hashlib</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>sha256</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>proof_input</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>hexdigest</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>  </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Placeholder ZKP</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">return</span><span> zkp
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Normalize output</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">def</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">normalize_response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">str</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">&gt;</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">str</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">return</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"\n"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>join</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">sorted</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>line</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>strip</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">for</span><span> line </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">in</span><span> response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>splitlines</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">if</span><span> line</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>strip</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Write output deterministically</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">def</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">write_output</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>filename</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">str</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> content</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">str</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">with</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">open</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>filename</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"w"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> encoding</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"utf-8"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> newline</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"\n"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">as</span><span> f</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>        f</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>write</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>content</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Feedback loop with ZKPs</span><span>
</span><span>current_input </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Name the top 5 cities in the world by population as of </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">FIXED_DATE</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">."</span><span>
</span><span style=""></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">for</span><span style=""> i </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">in</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">range</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">2</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Run local LLM inference</span><span>
</span><span>    response </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> local_llm_inference</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>current_input</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>    normalized </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> normalize_response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>    output_hash </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> hashlib</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>sha256</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>normalized</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>encode</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>hexdigest</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span>
<span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Generate ZKP</span><span>
</span><span>    zkp </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> generate_zkp</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>current_input</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> normalized</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span>
<span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Save output with proof</span><span>
</span><span>    output_content </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>
</span><span>        </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Step </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">i</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);"> Prompt: </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">current_input</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\n"</span><span>
</span><span>        </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Normalized Response:\n</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">normalized</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\n"</span><span>
</span><span>        </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Hash: </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">output_hash</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\n"</span><span>
</span><span>        </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"ZKP: </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">zkp</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\n"</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>    filename </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"output_step_</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">i</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">.txt"</span><span>
</span><span>    write_output</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>filename</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> output_content</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">print</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Wrote </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">filename</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span>
<span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Feed back</span><span>
</span><span>    current_input </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> normalized
</span></code></pre></div></div><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-b88u0q" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234); display: block;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Output Example (</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-z32n2g r-z2wwpe r-1hkscgl r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">output_step_0.txt</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">)</span></span></span></div><div class="css-175oi2r r-1b5gpbm r-dnmrzs r-1yx7oqi"><div class="css-175oi2r" data-testid="markdown-code-block"><div class="css-175oi2r r-1awozwy r-g2wdr4 r-1fs5b29 r-1idry7j r-6413gk r-43g30s r-l4nmg1 r-1u658rm r-2dysd3 r-vmopo1 r-13qz1uu r-gtdqiz r-1fhadnw r-184en5c"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-rjixqe r-16dba41 r-1aiqnjv r-n6v787" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"></div><div class="css-175oi2r r-1ybcz0z"></div></div><pre style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);
