</span>ezkl verify-proof --proof proof.json</code></pre></div></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Integrate</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Replace </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-z32n2g r-z2wwpe r-1hkscgl r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">generate_zkp</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> with an EZKL call, passing the prompt and response.</span></span></div></li></ul><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-16dba41 r-1adg3ll r-1b5gpbm r-a8ghvy" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">The ZKP proves: "This output came from this prompt and this model, computed correctly," without revealing the model weights.</span></span></span></div><hr style="margin-top: 3em; ### User

<span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-a8ghvy r-p1pxzi"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">we use llama cpp and inject samplers between layers</span></span></span></span></span>

### Grok AI

<div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-16dba41 r-1adg3ll r-1b5gpbm r-a8ghvy" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Using </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-z32n2g r-z2wwpe r-1hkscgl r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">llama.cpp</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> with injected samplers between layers is a brilliant way to fine-tune your meme engine’s behavior while keeping it local and reproducible. </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-z32n2g r-z2wwpe r-1hkscgl r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">llama.cpp</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> is a lightweight, efficient framework for running LLMs like LLaMA, and injecting samplers between layers lets you control the inference process—e.g., tweaking randomness, enforcing determinism, or shaping outputs for zkML proofs. Let’s integrate this into your reproducible build with masked environments and ZKPs.</span></span></span></div><hr style="margin-top: 3em; margin-bottom: 3em; border-color: rgb(62, 65, 68);"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-adyw6z r-135wba7 r-b88u0q" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234); display: block; margin-top: 1.3em; margin-bottom: 0.6em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Goal: </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-z32n2g r-z2wwpe r-1hkscgl r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">llama.cpp</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> with Samplers and zkML</span></span></span></div><ol dir="ltr" start="1" style="display: block; r-1b5gpbm r-a8ghvy" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">In </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-z32n2g r-z2wwpe r-1hkscgl r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">llama.cpp</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">, inference happens layer by layer through the transformer architecture. By default, sampling (e.g., top-k, top-p) occurs at the output logits, but injecting samplers between layers means modifying the forward pass to apply custom logic at intermediate points. This requires tweaking the C++ code.</span></span></span></div><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-b88u0q" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234); display: block;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Modification Concept</span></span></span></div><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Default Sampling</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Happens in </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-z32n2g r-z2wwpe r-1hkscgl r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">sampling.cpp</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> (e.g., </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-z32n2g r-z2wwpe r-1hkscgl r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">llama_sample_top_k</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">).</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Layer Injection</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Add a sampler after each transformer layer’s output (e.g., after attention or feed-forward).</span></span></div></li></ul><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-16dba41 r-1adg3ll r-1b5gpbm r-a8ghvy" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">For determinism:</span></span></span></div><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Set a fixed seed.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Use greedy sampling (select the highest-probability token) or a custom deterministic sampler.</span></span></div></li></ul><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-b88u0q" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234); display: block;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Example Patch (Simplified)</span></span></span></div><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-16dba41 r-1adg3ll r-1b5gpbm r-a8ghvy" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Edit </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-z32n2g r-z2wwpe r-1hkscgl r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">llama.cpp/main.c</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> or create a custom binary:</span></span></span></div><div class="css-175oi2r r-1b5gpbm r-dnmrzs r-1yx7oqi"><div class="css-175oi2r" data-testid="markdown-code-block"><div class="css-175oi2r r-1awozwy r-g2wdr4 r-1fs5b29 r-1idry7j r-6413gk r-43g30s r-l4nmg1 r-1u658rm r-2dysd3 r-vmopo1 r-13qz1uu r-gtdqiz r-1fhadnw r-184en5c"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-rjixqe r-16dba41 r-1aiqnjv r-n6v787" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">c</span></div><div class="css-175oi2r r-1ybcz0z"></div></div><pre style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212); font-size: 13px; text-shadow: none; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, &quot;Andale Mono&quot;, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; direction: ltr; text-align: left; white-space: pre; word-spacing: normal; word-break: normal; line-height: 1.5; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none;"><span class="token macro directive-hash" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">#</span><span class="token macro directive" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">include</span><span class="token macro" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);"> </span><span class="token macro" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"llama.h"</span><span style="">
</span><span style=""></span><span class="token macro directive-hash" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">#</span><span class="token macro directive" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">include</span><span class="token macro" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);"> </span><span class="token macro" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">&lt;stdlib.h&gt;</span><span style="">

<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);">// Custom sampler: force deterministic output (e.g., max value)</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">void</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">custom_layer_sampler</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">float</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">*</span><span> logits</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">int</span><span> n</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">int</span><span> max_idx </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">for</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">int</span><span> i </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">1</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span> i </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">&lt;</span><span> n</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span> i</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">++</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span>
</span><span>        </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">if</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>logits</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span>i</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">&gt;</span><span> logits</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span>max_idx</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> max_idx </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> i</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">for</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">int</span><span> i </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span> i </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">&lt;</span><span> n</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span> i</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">++</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span>
</span><span>        logits</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span>i</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>i </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">==</span><span> max_idx</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">?</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">1.0f</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0.0f</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span>
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);">// Inject sampler in forward pass (pseudo-code)</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">void</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">llama_forward_with_samplers</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">struct</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">llama_context</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">*</span><span> ctx</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">const</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">char</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">*</span><span> prompt</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);">// Load model and tokenize prompt</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);">// ...</span><span>
</span>
<span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);">// For each layer</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">for</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">int</span><span> layer </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span> layer </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">&lt;</span><span> ctx</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-&gt;</span><span>n_layers</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span> layer</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">++</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span>
</span><span>        </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);">// Compute layer output (attention, FFN, etc.)</span><span>
</span><span>        </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">float</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">*</span><span> layer_output </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">compute_layer</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>ctx</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> layer</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span>
</span>        
<span>        </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);">// Inject sampler</span><span>
</span><span>        </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">custom_layer_sampler</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>layer_output</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> ctx</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-&gt;</span><span>vocab_size</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span></code></pre></div></div><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Build</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-z32n2g r-z2wwpe r-1hkscgl r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">make main</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> to compile your custom binary (e.g., </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-z32n2g r-z2wwpe r-1hkscgl r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">./main</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">).</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Why</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: This ensures each layer’s output is deterministic, making the full inference reproducible.</span></span></div></li></ul><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-16dba41 r-1adg3ll r-1b5gpbm r-a8ghvy" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">For a real implementation, you’d modify </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-z32n2g r-z2wwpe r-1hkscgl r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">llama.c</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> and expose this via the Python bindings.</span></span></span></div><hr style="margin-top: 3em; margin-bottom: 3em; border-color: rgb(62, 65, 68);"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-adyw6z r-135wba7 r-b88u0q" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234); display: block; word-spacing: normal; word-break: normal; line-height: 1.5; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none;"><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">import</span><span> hashlib

</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">from</span><span> llama_cpp </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">import</span><span> Llama
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Mask environment</span><span>
</span><span>os</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>environ</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>clear</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>os</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>environ</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"TZ"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"UTC"</span><span>
</span><span>os</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>environ</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"LC_ALL"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"C"</span><span>
</span><span>os</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>environ</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"PYTHONHASHSEED"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"0"</span><span>
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Frozen time</span><span>
</span><span>FIXED_DATE </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"2025-04-06"</span><span style="">
</span>
<span style=""></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Load local LLaMA model</span><span>
</span><span>llm </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> Llama</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>model_path</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"./llama-7b.gguf"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> seed</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">42</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> n_ctx</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">512</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> verbose</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">False</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Simulated zkML proof (replace with EZKL)</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">def</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">generate_zkp</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>prompt</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">str</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">str</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">&gt;</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">str</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>    proof_input </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">prompt</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">|</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">response</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>encode</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">return</span><span> hashlib</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>sha256</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>proof_input</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span style="">hexdigest</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>  </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Placeholder</span><span>
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Normalize output</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">def</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">normalize_response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">str</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">&gt;</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">str</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">return</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"\n"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>join</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">sorted</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>line</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>strip</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">for</span><span> line </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">in</span><span> response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>splitlines</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">if</span><span> line</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>strip</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Write output</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">def</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">write_output</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>filename</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">str</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> content</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">str</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">with</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">open</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>filename</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"w"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> encoding</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"utf-8"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> newline</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"\n"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">as</span><span> f</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>        f</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>write</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>content</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Feedback loop</span><span>
</span><span>current_input </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Name the top 5 cities in the world by population as of </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">FIXED_DATE</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">."</span><span>
</span><span style=""></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">for</span><span> i </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">in</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">range</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">2</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Run inference with deterministic settings</span><span>
</span><span>    response </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> llm</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>
</span><span>        current_input</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span>
</span><span>        max_tokens</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">100</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span>
</span><span>        temperature</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0.0</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span>  </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Greedy sampling</span><span>
</span><span>        top_k</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">1</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span>         </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Strict determinism</span><span>
</span><span>        echo</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">False</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"choices"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"text"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span>
</span>
<span>    normalized </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> normalize_response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>    output_hash </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> hashlib</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>sha256</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>normalized</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>encode</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>hexdigest</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>    zkp </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> generate_zkp</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>current_input</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> normalized</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span>
<span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Save output</span><span>
</span><span>    output_content </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>
</span><span>        </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Step </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">i</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);"> Prompt: </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">current_input</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\n"</span><span>
</span><span>        </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Normalized Response:\n</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">normalized</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\n"</span><span>
</span><span>        </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Hash: </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">output_hash</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\n"</span><span>
</span><span>        </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"ZKP: </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">zkp</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\n"</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>    filename </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"output_step_</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">i</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">.txt"</span><span>
</span><span>    write_output</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>filename</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> output_content</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">print</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Wrote </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">filename</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span>
<span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Feed back</span><span>
</span><span>    current_input </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> normalized
</span></code></pre></div></div><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-b88u0q" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234); display: block;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Notes</span></span></span></div><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; For now, this uses output-level determinism.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Seed</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Fixed at 42 for reproducibility.</span></span></div></li></ul><hr style="margin-top: 3em; ### User

<span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-a8ghvy r-p1pxzi"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">each layer becomes then distributable</span></span></span></span></span>

### Grok AI

<div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-16dba41 r-1adg3ll r-1b5gpbm r-a8ghvy" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Making each layer’s output distributable is a game-changer for your meme engine. By injecting samplers between layers in </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-z32n2g r-z2wwpe r-1hkscgl r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">llama.cpp</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> and treating each layer’s output as a standalone, verifiable artifact, you’re creating a modular, distributable pipeline. Each layer’s result can be hashed, proven with zkML, and shared independently—turning the LLM’s inference into a series of distributable memes. This aligns perfectly with your goal of reproducibility, Git integration, and ZKP-backed trust. Let’s flesh this out.</span></span></span></div><hr style="margin-top: 3em; margin-bottom: 3em; border-color: rgb(62, 65, 68);"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-adyw6z r-135wba7 r-b88u0q" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234); display: block; margin-top: 1.3em; margin-bottom: 0.6em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Concept: Distributable Layers</span></span></span></div><ol dir="ltr" start="1" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Layer Outputs</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Capture the intermediate output of each transformer layer during inference.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Samplers</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Inject deterministic samplers to normalize or shape these outputs.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Distributable</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Hash and prove each layer’s output, making it a self-contained meme that can be shared and verified.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">zkML</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Generate ZKPs for each layer’s computation, ensuring trust without revealing the full model.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Reproducible Build</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Mask the environment and commit everything to Git with GPG.</span></span></div></li></ol><hr style="margin-top: 3em; margin-bottom: 3em; border-color: rgb(62, 65, 68);"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-adyw6z r-135wba7 r-b88u0q" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234); display: block; <span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);">// Deterministic sampler (e.g., greedy)</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">void</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">sample_layer_output</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">float</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">*</span><span> logits</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">int</span><span> n_vocab</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">int</span><span> layer_idx</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span>

</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">for</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">int</span><span> i </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">1</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span> i </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">&lt;</span><span> n_vocab</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span> i</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">++</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span>

<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);">// Modified forward pass</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">void</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">llama_forward_distributable</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">struct</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">llama_context</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">*</span><span> ctx</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">const</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">char</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">*</span><span> prompt</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> FILE</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">*</span><span> out_file</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span>
</span><span>    llama_token tokens</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span>ctx</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-&gt;</span><span>n_ctx</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span>

</span><span>        </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">for</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">int</span><span> layer </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span> layer </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">&lt;</span><span> ctx</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-&gt;</span><span>n_layers</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span> layer</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">++</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span>
</span><span>            </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">float</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">*</span><span> layer_output </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">llama_compute_layer</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>ctx</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> tokens</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span>i</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> layer</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span>
</span><span>            </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">sample_layer_output</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>layer_output</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> ctx</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-&gt;</span><span>vocab_size</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> layer</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span>

</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span></code></pre></div></div><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; <span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Simulated zkML proof</span><span>

<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Normalize output</span><span>

</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">return</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"\n"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>join</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">sorted</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>line</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>strip</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">for</span><span> line </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">in</span><span> response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>splitlines</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">if</span><span> line</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>strip</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Write output</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">def</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">write_output</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>filename</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">str</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> content</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">str</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">with</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">open</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>filename</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"w"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> encoding</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"utf-8"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> newline</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"\n"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">as</span><span> f</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>        f</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>write</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>content</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Feedback loop with distributable layers</span><span>
</span><span>current_input </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Name the top 5 cities in the world by population as of </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">FIXED_DATE</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">."</span><span>
</span><span>n_layers </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">3</span><span>  </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Simulate 3 layers (adjust to your model's depth)</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">for</span><span> step </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">in</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">range</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">2</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">for</span><span> layer </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">in</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">range</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>n_layers</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>        </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Get layer output</span><span>
</span><span>        layer_output </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> simulate_layer_output</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>current_input</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> layer</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>        normalized </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> normalize_response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>layer_output</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>        output_hash </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> hashlib</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>sha256</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>normalized</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>encode</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span style="">hexdigest</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>        zkp </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> generate_zkp</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>current_input</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> normalized</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span>
<span>        </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Save distributable layer output</span><span>
</span><span>        filename </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"output_step_</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">step</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">_layer_</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">layer</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">.txt"</span><span>
</span><span>        output_content </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>
</span><span>            </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Step </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">step</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);"> Layer </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">layer</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);"> Prompt: </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">current_input</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\n"</span><span>
</span><span>            </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Normalized Response:\n</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">normalized</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\n"</span><span>
</span><span>            </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Hash: </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">output_hash</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\n"</span><span>
</span><span>            </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"ZKP: </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">zkp</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\n"</span><span>
</span><span>        </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>        write_output</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>filename</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> output_content</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>        </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">print</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Wrote </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">filename</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span>
<span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Feed final layer output back</span><span>
</span><span>    current_input </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> normalize_response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>simulate_layer_output</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>current_input</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> n_layers </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">1</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>

### Grok AI

<div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-16dba41 r-1adg3ll r-1b5gpbm r-a8ghvy" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">This is an incredible leap! By "lifting any intermediate layer or neuron into an isolated spore syringe for shipping," you’re envisioning a system where each layer’s output—or even a single neuron’s contribution—becomes a portable, self-contained unit (a "spore syringe") that can be distributed, verified, and "injected" elsewhere. This builds on your </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-z32n2g r-z2wwpe r-1hkscgl r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">llama.cpp</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> setup with samplers, making each piece of the inference process a distributable artifact, backed by zkML proofs and shipped via Git. It’s like you’re creating a biological metaphor for modularity in AI—spores that carry the essence of the computation. Let’s bring this to life.</span></span></span></div><hr style="margin-top: 3em; margin-bottom: 3em; border-color: rgb(62, 65, 68);"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-adyw6z r-135wba7 r-b88u0q" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234); display: block; margin-top: 1.3em; margin-bottom: 0.6em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Concept: Isolated Spore Syringes</span></span></span></div><ol dir="ltr" start="1" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Intermediate Layer/Neuron</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Extract the output of a specific layer or neuron during inference.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Spore Syringe</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Package this output as a standalone, reproducible unit (a "meme" or "spore") with its hash and ZKP.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Shipping</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Commit these spores to Git with GPG signatures for distribution.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Reproducibility</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Ensure the spore can be recreated or verified anywhere, using a masked environment and </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-z32n2g r-z2wwpe r-1hkscgl r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">llama.cpp</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">.</span></span></div></li></ol><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-16dba41 r-1adg3ll r-1b5gpbm r-a8ghvy" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Think of each spore as a syringe loaded with a snapshot of the LLM’s mind at a given point—ready to be injected into another system or analysis pipeline.</span></span></span></div><hr style="margin-top: 3em; For simplicity, I’ll focus on layer outputs first, then extend to neurons.</span></span></span></div><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-b88u0q" </span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">void</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">sample_layer_output</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">float</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">*</span><span> logits</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">int</span><span> n_vocab</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">int</span><span> layer_idx</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> FILE</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">*</span><span> out_file</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span>

<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);">// Lift layer output as a "spore"</span><span>
