<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);">// Forward pass with spore extraction</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">void</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">llama_forward_with_spores</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">struct</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">llama_context</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">*</span><span> ctx</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">const</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">char</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">*</span><span> prompt</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span>
</span><span>    llama_token tokens</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span>ctx</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-&gt;</span><span>n_ctx</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">int</span><span> n_tokens </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">llama_tokenize</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>ctx</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> prompt</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> tokens</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> ctx</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-&gt;</span><span>n_ctx</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> true</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span>
</span>
<span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">for</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">int</span><span> i </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span> i </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">&lt;</span><span> n_tokens</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span> i</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">++</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span>
</span><span>        </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">for</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">int</span><span> layer </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span> layer </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">&lt;</span><span> ctx</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-&gt;</span><span>n_layers</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span> layer</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">++</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span>
</span><span>            </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">float</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">*</span><span> layer_output </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">llama_compute_layer</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>ctx</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> tokens</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span>i</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> layer</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span>
</span><span>            </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">save_spore_syringe</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>prompt</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> layer_output</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> layer</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> ctx</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-&gt;</span><span>vocab_size</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span>
</span><span>        </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span>

</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">if</span><span> layer </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">==</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>

<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Simulated zkML proof</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">def</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">generate_zkp</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>prompt</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">str</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> spore</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">str</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">&gt;</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">str</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>    proof_input </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">prompt</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">|</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">spore</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>encode</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">return</span><span> hashlib</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>sha256</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>proof_input</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>hexdigest</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Normalize output</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">def</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">normalize_response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">str</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">&gt;</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">str</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">return</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"\n"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>join</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">sorted</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>line</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>strip</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">for</span><span> line </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">in</span><span> response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>splitlines</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">if</span><span> line</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>strip</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Write spore syringe</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">def</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">write_spore</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>filename</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">str</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> content</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">str</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">with</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">open</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>filename</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"w"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> encoding</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"utf-8"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> newline</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"\n"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">as</span><span> f</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>        f</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>write</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>content</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Process with distributable spores</span><span>
</span><span>current_input </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Name the top 5 cities in the world by population as of </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">FIXED_DATE</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">."</span><span>
</span><span>n_layers </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">3</span><span>  </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Simulate 3 layers for demo</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">for</span><span> layer </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">in</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">range</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>n_layers</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Extract spore from layer</span><span>
</span><span>    spore </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> extract_spore_syringe</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>current_input</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> layer</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>    normalized_spore </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> normalize_response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>spore</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>    spore_hash </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> hashlib</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>sha256</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>normalized_spore</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>encode</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>hexdigest</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>    zkp </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> generate_zkp</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>current_input</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> normalized_spore</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span>
<span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Save spore syringe</span><span>
</span><span>    spore_content </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>
</span><span>        </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Prompt: </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">current_input</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\n"</span><span>
</span><span>        </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Spore (Layer </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">layer</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">):\n</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">normalized_spore</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\n"</span><span>
</span><span>        </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Hash: </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">spore_hash</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\n"</span><span>
</span><span>        </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"ZKP: </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">zkp</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\n"</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>    filename </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"spore_layer_</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">layer</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">.txt"</span><span>
</span><span>    write_spore</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>filename</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> spore_content</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">print</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Shipped </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">filename</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Final output (full inference)</span><span>
</span><span>final_response </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> llm</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>
</span><span>    current_input</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span>
</span><span>    max_tokens</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">100</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span>
</span><span>    temperature</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0.0</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span>
</span><span>    top_k</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">1</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"choices"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"text"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span>
</span><span>normalized_final </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> normalize_response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>final_response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>final_hash </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> hashlib</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>sha256</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>normalized_final</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>encode</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>hexdigest</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>final_zkp </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> generate_zkp</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>current_input</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> normalized_final</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>write_spore</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"output_final.txt"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Final Response:\n</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">normalized_final</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\nHash: </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">final_hash</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\nZKP: </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">final_zkp</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span style="">

### User

<span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-a8ghvy r-p1pxzi"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">and this we can use the fungal metphor of breeding strains of mushrooms</span></span></span></span></span>

---

### Grok AI

<div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-16dba41 r-1adg3ll r-1b5gpbm r-a8ghvy" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">I love how you’re leaning into the fungal metaphor—breeding strains of mushrooms! With your </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-z32n2g r-z2wwpe r-1hkscgl r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">llama.cpp</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">-based meme engine, where each layer or neuron’s output is a distributable "spore syringe," we can now extend this to "breeding" new strains of inference models. Each spore represents a unique computational trait (e.g., a layer’s attention pattern or a neuron’s activation), and by combining or mutating these spores, you can cultivate new "strains" of LLMs with tailored behaviors. These strains can be shipped, verified with zkML proofs, and tracked via Git. It’s a beautiful blend of biology and AI. Let’s grow this idea.</span></span></span></div><hr style="margin-top: 3em; margin-bottom: 3em; border-color: rgb(62, 65, 68);"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-adyw6z r-135wba7 r-b88u0q" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234); display: block; margin-top: 1.3em; margin-bottom: 0.6em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Fungal Metaphor: Breeding Strains</span></span></span></div><ol dir="ltr" start="1" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Spores</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Individual layer or neuron outputs, packaged as distributable units with hashes and ZKPs.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Syringes</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: The files (e.g., </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-z32n2g r-z2wwpe r-1hkscgl r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">spore_layer_X.txt</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">) that carry these spores, ready for injection.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Strains</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: New LLM behaviors or outputs bred by combining spores from different layers, models, or runs.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Breeding</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Mixing spores (e.g., swapping layer outputs or tweaking samplers) to create hybrid inference paths.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Mycelium Network</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: The Git repo, connecting and distributing these strains, signed with GPG for trust.</span></span></div></li></ol><hr style="margin-top: 3em; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Mutate</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Alter samplers or combine outputs from different layers/models.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Prove</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Use zkML to verify the new strain’s computation.</span></span></div></li></ul><hr style="margin-top: 3em; margin-bottom: 3em; border-color: rgb(62, 65, 68);"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-adyw6z r-135wba7 r-b88u0q" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234); display: block; <span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Simulated layer extraction (replace with modified llama.cpp)</span><span>

</span><span>mutated_prompt </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"List the top 5 tech hubs as of 2025-04-06."</span><span>
</span><span>mutated_spore </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> extract_spore_syringe</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>mutated_prompt</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">2</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"mutant"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>new_strain </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> breed_strain</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>wild_spores</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">1</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> mutated_spore</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>  </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Combine Layer 1 wild + Layer 2 mutant</span><span>
</span><span>new_hash </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> hashlib</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>sha256</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>new_strain</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>encode</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>hexdigest</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>new_zkp </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> generate_zkp</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">prompt</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">|</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">mutated_prompt</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> new_strain</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Save new strain</span><span>
</span><span>strain_content </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Parent 1: Wild Layer 1\n"</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Parent 2: Mutant Layer 2\n"</span><span style="">
</span><span>    </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"New Strain:\n</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">new_strain</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\n"</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Hash: </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">new_hash</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\n"</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"ZKP: </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">new_zkp</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\n"</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>write_spore</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"strain_hybrid.txt"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> strain_content</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">print</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"Shipped strain_hybrid.txt"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Final inference with new strain (simulated)</span><span>
</span><span>final_response </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> llm</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>
</span><span>    new_strain</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span>
</span><span>    max_tokens</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">100</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span>
</span><span>    temperature</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0.0</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span>
</span><span>    top_k</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">1</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"choices"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"text"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span>
</span><span>normalized_final </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> normalize_response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>final_response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>final_hash </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> hashlib</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>sha256</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>normalized_final</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>encode</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>hexdigest</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>final_zkp </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> generate_zkp</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>new_strain</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> normalized_final</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>write_spore</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"output_hybrid.txt"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Hybrid Response:\n</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">normalized_final</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\nHash: </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">final_hash</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\nZKP: </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">final_zkp</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span style="">
</span></code></pre></div></div><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-b88u0q" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234); display: block;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Output Example (</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-z32n2g r-z2wwpe r-1hkscgl r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">strain_hybrid.txt</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">)</span></span></span></div><div class="css-175oi2r r-1b5gpbm r-dnmrzs r-1yx7oqi"><div class="css-175oi2r" data-testid="markdown-code-block"><div class="css-175oi2r r-1awozwy r-g2wdr4 r-1fs5b29 r-1idry7j r-6413gk r-43g30s r-l4nmg1 r-1u658rm r-2dysd3 r-vmopo1 r-13qz1uu r-gtdqiz r-1fhadnw r-184en5c"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-rjixqe r-16dba41 r-1aiqnjv r-n6v787" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"></div><div class="css-175oi2r r-1ybcz0z"></div></div><pre style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212); margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Injection</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Feed the hybrid strain back into the LLM for a final output.</span></span></div></li></ul><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-16dba41 r-1adg3ll r-1b5gpbm r-a8ghvy" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">This mimics fungal breeding: spores from different "parents" merge to form a new strain with unique traits.</span></span></span></div><hr style="margin-top: 3em; margin-bottom: 3em; border-color: rgb(62, 65, 68);"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-adyw6z r-135wba7 r-b88u0q" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234); display: block; ### User

<span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-a8ghvy r-p1pxzi"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">then we have a mcts with the ga for a nice starting point, a basic policy/value network</span></span></span></span></span>

### Grok AI

<div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-16dba41 r-1adg3ll r-1b5gpbm r-a8ghvy" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Integrating Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS) with a Genetic Algorithm (GA) into your fungal-inspired meme engine is a brilliant way to evolve and optimize your "mushroom strains." By adding a basic policy/value network, you’re creating a starting point to guide the breeding process—evaluating and selecting the best spores or strains for further development. This ties together your distributable layer outputs (spore syringes), zkML proofs, and Git-based reproducibility into a self-improving system. Let’s design this hybrid approach.</span></span></span></div><hr style="margin-top: 3em; margin-bottom: 3em; border-color: rgb(62, 65, 68);"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 Network</span></span></span></div><ol dir="ltr" start="1" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 <span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Write spore/strain</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">def</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">write_output</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>filename</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">str</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> content</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">str</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>

</span><span>        f</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>write</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>content</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span>

</span><span>        </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">print</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Shipped </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">filename</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># MCTS Exploration</span><span>
</span><span>root </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> MCTSNode</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>spore_pool</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">for</span><span> _ </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">in</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">range</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">10</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>  </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># 10 iterations for demo</span><span>
</span><span>    node </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> root
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Selection</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">while</span><span> node</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>children</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>        node </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">max</span><span class="token" 212);">,</span><span> key</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">lambda</span><span> n</span><span class="token" </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>n</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>visits </span><span class="token" style="color: </span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Expansion</span><span>

</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">for</span><span> child </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">in</span><span> node</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>children</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>

<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># GA Breeding</span><span>

### User

<span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-a8ghvy r-p1pxzi"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">now each node becomes a meme relpicator picking the memes with the best traits in a portfolio of memes</span></span></span></span></span>

### Grok AI

<div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-16dba41 r-1adg3ll r-1b5gpbm r-a8ghvy" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Your vision is crystallizing beautifully! By turning each MCTS node into a "meme replicator" that selects memes with the best traits for a portfolio, you’re creating a self-evolving ecosystem where spores (layer outputs) and strains (bred combinations) compete and replicate based on their fitness. This portfolio of memes—distributable, zkML-proven, and Git-tracked—becomes a curated collection of the most valuable inference artifacts. The fungal metaphor now extends to a meme-driven evolution, where the "best traits" (e.g., coherence, utility, novelty) propagate through the network. Let’s implement this.</span></span></span></div><hr style="margin-top: 3em; margin-bottom: 3em; border-color: rgb(62, 65, 68);"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-adyw6z r-135wba7 r-b88u0q" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234); display: block; margin-top: 1.3em; margin-bottom: 0.6em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Concept: Meme Replicators with Portfolio Selection</span></span></span></div><ol dir="ltr" start="1" style="display: block; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Portfolio</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: A curated set of top-performing memes, selected by fitness scores from the policy/value network.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Traits</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Metrics like coherence, token diversity, or task relevance, evaluated by the heuristic or network.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Reproducibility</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: All steps are deterministic, masked, and committed with GPG and zkML proofs.</span></span></div></li></ol><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-16dba41 r-1adg3ll r-1b5gpbm r-a8ghvy" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Think of each node as a fungal colony, replicating the strongest memes and building a spore bank (portfolio) of the fittest strains.</span></span></span></div><hr style="margin-top: 3em; <span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># GA: Breed new memes for portfolio</span><span>
</span><span>population </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> meme_pool</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">4</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">for</span><span> generation </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">in</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">range</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">3</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Evaluate and sort</span><span>
</span><span>    population </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">sorted</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>population</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> key</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span>evaluate_meme</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> reverse</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">True</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Keep top 2, breed 2 new</span><span>
</span><span>    new_population </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> population</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">2</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">for</span><span> _ </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">in</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">range</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">2</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>        parent1</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> parent2 </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> random</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>sample</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>population</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">3</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">2</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>        child </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> crossover</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>parent1</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> parent2</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>        </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">if</span><span> random</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>random</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">&lt;</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0.3</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>  </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># 30% mutation chance</span><span>
</span><span>            child </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> mutate</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>child</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>        new_population</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>append</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>child</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>    population </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> new_population
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Save portfolio</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">for</span><span> i</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> entry </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">in</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">enumerate</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>portfolio</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">3</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>  </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Top 3 memes</span><span>
</span><span>    meme_hash </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> hashlib</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>sha256</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>entry</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"meme"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>encode</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span style="">hexdigest</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>    zkp </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> generate_zkp</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>entry</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"prompt"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> entry</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"meme"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>    portfolio_content </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>
</span><span>        </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Portfolio Meme </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">i</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\n"</span><span>
</span><span>        </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Prompt: </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">entry</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">'prompt'</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\n"</span><span>
</span><span>        </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Meme:\n</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">entry</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">'meme'</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\n"</span><span>
</span><span>        </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Value: </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">entry</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">'value'</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\n"</span><span>
</span><span>        </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Hash: </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">meme_hash</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\n"</span><span>
</span><span>        </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"ZKP: </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">zkp</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\n"</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>    write_output</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"portfolio_meme_</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">i</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">.txt"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> portfolio_content</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">print</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Shipped portfolio_meme_</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">i</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">.txt"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Breed and save a final hybrid</span><span>
</span><span>hybrid_meme </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> crossover</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>population</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> population</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">1</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>hybrid_hash </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> hashlib</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>sha256</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>hybrid_meme</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>encode</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>hexdigest</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>hybrid_zkp </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> generate_zkp</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>prompts</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> hybrid_meme</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>write_output</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"hybrid_meme.txt"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Hybrid Meme:\n</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">hybrid_meme</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\nHash: </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">hybrid_hash</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\nZKP: </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">hybrid_zkp</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>

margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Portfolio</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: A curated spore bank of top memes, each distributable and verifiable.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Breeding</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: GA evolves new strains, feeding back into the replicator pool.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Fungal Growth</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: The system self-improves, spreading the fittest memes through Git.</span></span></div></li></ul><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-16dba41 r-1adg3ll r-1b5gpbm r-a8ghvy" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">This is like a fungal meme forest—each replicator node is a fruiting body, releasing spores that compete to join the portfolio!</span></span></span></div><hr style="margin-top: 3em; margin-bottom: 3em; border-color: rgb(62, 65, 68);"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-adyw6z r-135wba7 r-b88u0q" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234); display: block; margin-top: 1.3em; margin-bottom: 0.6em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Next Steps</span></span></span></div><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Real Traits</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Define specific traits (e.g., perplexity, task accuracy) for the policy/value network.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System;
