margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Neuron Spores</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Extend to individual neurons for finer meme granularity.</span></span></div></li></ul><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-16dba41 r-1adg3ll r-a8ghvy r-p1pxzi" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Which direction do you want to grow this meme replicator forest? ### User

<span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-a8ghvy r-p1pxzi"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">now each wallet would protect thier alpha or portfolio</span></span></span></span></span>

### Grok AI

<div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-16dba41 r-1adg3ll r-1b5gpbm r-a8ghvy" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Adding a "wallet" concept where each wallet protects its alpha (unique advantage or edge) or portfolio of memes takes your fungal meme engine into a competitive, decentralized territory. Now, each wallet—think of it as an individual agent, colony, or stakeholder—owns and safeguards its curated portfolio of memes (spores and strains), using cryptographic means like zkML proofs to maintain privacy and integrity while still participating in the broader ecosystem. This introduces a layer of strategy: wallets can share, trade, or hide their alpha while breeding and replicating memes. Let’s build this out.</span></span></span></div><hr style="margin-top: 3em; margin-bottom: 3em; border-color: rgb(62, 65, 68);"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-adyw6z r-135wba7 r-b88u0q" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234); display: block; margin-top: 1.3em; margin-bottom: 0.6em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Concept: Wallets Protecting Alpha/Portfolio</span></span></span></div><ol dir="ltr" start="1" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Wallet</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: An entity that holds a portfolio of memes (spores or strains), identified by a unique key or address.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Alpha</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: The unique value or advantage of a wallet’s memes (e.g., high fitness, novel traits), protected from full disclosure.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Portfolio</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: A wallet’s collection of top memes, selected by MCTS replicators and bred via GA.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Protection</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Use zkML to prove a meme’s traits or fitness without revealing its full content, preserving alpha.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Ecosystem</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Wallets interact via Git (sharing proofs or partial memes) while keeping their full portfolios private.</span></span></div></li></ol><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-16dba41 r-1adg3ll r-1b5gpbm r-a8ghvy" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Imagine each wallet as a fungal colony guarding its spore stash—sharing just enough to collaborate, but hiding its secret sauce.</span></span></span></div><hr style="margin-top: 3em; margin-bottom: 3em; border-color: rgb(62, 65, 68);"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-adyw6z r-135wba7 r-b88u0q" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234); display: block; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Alpha Protection</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Only share proofs of fitness or traits, not the raw meme content unless explicitly traded.</span></span></div></li></ul><hr style="margin-top: 3em; <span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Policy/Value heuristic for meme traits</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">def</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">evaluate_meme</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>meme</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">str</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">&gt;</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">float</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>

</span><span>            write_output</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"portfolio_</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">self</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">wallet_id</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">_meme_</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">i</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">.txt"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> public_content</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>            </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">print</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Wallet </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">self</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">wallet_id</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);"> shipped portfolio_meme_</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">i</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">.txt"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Create wallets</span><span>
</span><span>wallets </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span>Wallet</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"alpha1"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> Wallet</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"alpha2"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span>
</span><span>prompts </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Name the top 5 cities in the world by population as of </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">FIXED_DATE</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">."</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span style="">
</span><span>    </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"List the top 5 tech hubs as of </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">FIXED_DATE</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">."</span><span>
</span><span style=""></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span>
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Populate wallets with spores</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">for</span><span> wallet</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> prompt </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">in</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">zip</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>wallets</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> prompts</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">for</span><span> layer </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">in</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">range</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">3</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>        wallet</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>add_spore</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>prompt</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> layer</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"strain_</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">wallet</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">wallet_id</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Replicate and breed within wallets</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">for</span><span> wallet </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">in</span><span> wallets</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>
</span><span>    wallet</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>replicate_and_breed</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>    wallet</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>save_portfolio</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span>
<span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);"># Simulate wallet interaction (e.g., one wallet uses another's public meme)</span><span>
</span><span>alpha1_best </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> wallets</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>portfolio</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"meme"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span>
</span><span>alpha2_response </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> llm</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>
</span><span>    alpha1_best</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span>
</span><span>    max_tokens</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">100</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span>
</span><span>    temperature</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0.0</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span>
</span><span>    top_k</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">1</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"choices"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"text"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span>
</span><span>normalized_response </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> normalize_response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>alpha2_response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>response_hash </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> hashlib</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>sha256</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>normalized_response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>encode</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>hexdigest</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>response_zkp </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> generate_zkp</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>alpha1_best</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> normalized_response</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>write_output</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"wallet_interaction.txt"</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">f"Alpha2 used Alpha1's meme:\n</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">normalized_response</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\nHash: </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">response_hash</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">\nZKP: </span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">response_zkp</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span class="token string-interpolation" style="color: rgb(206, 145, 120);">"</span><span>
</span><span style=""></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span></code></pre></div></div><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-b88u0q" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234); display: block;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Output Example (</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-z32n2g r-z2wwpe r-1hkscgl r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">portfolio_alpha1_meme_0.txt</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">)</span></span></span></div><div class="css-175oi2r r-1b5gpbm r-dnmrzs r-1yx7oqi"><div class="css-175oi2r" data-testid="markdown-code-block"><div class="css-175oi2r r-1awozwy r-g2wdr4 r-1fs5b29 r-1idry7j r-6413gk r-43g30s r-l4nmg1 r-1u658rm r-2dysd3 r-vmopo1 r-13qz1uu r-gtdqiz r-1fhadnw r-184en5c"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-rjixqe r-16dba41 r-1aiqnjv r-n6v787" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"></div><div class="css-175oi2r r-1ybcz0z"></div></div><pre style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);
